=\n4th 2011</a> - 13 Mar 12</li>=0A</ul>=0A<br />=0A<h3>Our offices in the wor=\nld</h3>=0A<a href=3D\"/locations/offices\">=0A  <img src=3D\"/images/map.jpg\" =\nborder=3D\"0\" />=0A</a>=0A=0A=0A\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>=0A\t\t\t\t\t\t<div id=3D\"left_col\">=\n=0A\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<h1>Services</h1>=0D=0A<p>The firm is organized in <strong>three =\nkey branches</strong> with adapted technologies and processes.</p>=0D=0A<h4=\n>1. Audit</h4><p><ul><li>Under the authority of Daniel Nagle with the assis=\ntance of Marc Biquard, this branch performs financial audits and due dilige=\nnce work for medium size and major listed as well as for privatly owned com=\npanies.</li><li>It may also undertake or contribute to establishing interna=\nl control processes or SOX 404 audit processes and other kinds of services =\ninvolved, compliance of books and financials as well as establishing accoun=\nting policies for Groups in accordance with several standards (US GAAPs, IF=\nRS=E2=80=A6).</li></ul></p>=0D=0A=0D=0A<h4>2. Transaction Services</h4>=0D=\n=0A<p>The transaction services teams under the direction of Daniel Nagle, A=\ndriana Agbo and Jean-Fran=C3=A7ois Serval, and supported by dedicated teams=\n of professionals, are experienced in due diligence engagements to serve yo=\nur immediate or long terms requirements. Our teams have the necessary techn=\nical expertise derived from a large variety of industries and gained within=\n the United States and Europe. They will be a valuable tool in helping your=\n company make all crucial investment decisions. Working alongside investmen=\nt bankers and lawyers, we specialize in due diligence and VDD for private e=\nquity funds, we assist in restructuring companies and we help industrials t=\no purchase US or European businesses as a way to expand in those countries.=\n Our teams operate from the United States or Europe on a transnational scop=\ne therefore enabling delivery in several languages based upon your needs.</=\np>=0D=0A<h4>3. Accounting</h4>=0D=0A<p>Under the authority of Mlle Adriana =\nAgbo, this branch is able to provide full support to international companie=\ns for establishing financials, filling or auditing consolidation packages  =\nwith companies or head offices. It may  also undertake, on behalf of the cl=\nientele, some filing duties for the payroll and taxation.  It is very speci=\nalized in the follow up of US subsidiaries of non US companies from Europe.=\n</p>=0D=0A<h4>4. Special support divisions</h4><div class=3D\"box\"><p>To ope=\nrate the three operational branches, Constantin - Serval & Associes may hav=\ne the support of five lines of expertise.</p></div><div class=3D\"box\"><ul><=\nli> A separate <strong>software</strong> team may help the implementation o=\nf specific softwares for the clientele and/or connection with mother compan=\nies or factories of software  for the sales and delivery processes.</li>=0D=\n=0A<li> A <strong>tax</strong> team headed by Daniel Nagle will also be abl=\ne to cooperate with clients tax divisions or lawyers to make specific studi=\nes on expatriate filings, transfer pricing. Transfer pricing is a key topic=\n for all companies with international activities as subisidiaries of non US=\n entities operating in the US. A special team is conducting the studies to =\nsupport the transfer pricing policies adopted by clientele.</li>=0D=0A<li> =\nAn <strong>evaluation</strong> team headed by Guy Bernheim supports the all=\n practice as to impairment testing required by standards for the closing of=\n financials or price allocations in the course of reorganizations of acquis=\nition by a client.</li>=0D=0A<li> To ensure full <strong>compliance</strong=\n> with international group accounting policies and regulations in which the=\n mother company is located, special teams are able to operate accordingly e=\nither to US standards, ISA, or local european standards and specifications =\nfor US, French or other Europeans, Chinese... These international teams are=\n able also to provide global national services (ex: Tax for expatriates) on=\n an extended geographical base.</li><li>Throught its direct correspondants,=\n and its members in the US and other highly recognized accounting firms thr=\noughout the US, Constantin - Serval & Associes is able to provide its servi=\nces everywhere in the US and whatever is the size of the assignment for clo=\nsely held companies small or large, or public or listed ones. Constantin - =\nServal & Associes is a full service company.</li><li>Software &amp; Telecom=\nmunication <strong>security </strong>key issue is the security of systems, =\ntelecommunication &amp; access to systems. To issue the needed security com=\npliance with standards and needs of clients, a special team has been built =\nup with international level specialists. It is available to analyse clients=\n needs on special request or to support the audit teams.</li></ul></div><h4=\n>5. Global monitoring accounts from bank accounts</h4><p>Today, small and m=\nedium enterprises have to dedicate their energy to doing business and not a=\ndministration. Furthermore, they have to keep their hands on to the cash co=\nllection of their subsidiaries. Through their own bank system, we propose t=\no centralize all of their transactions abroad into a unified chart of accou=\nnts that the existing financial structure can handle after the current coll=\nections and disbursements have been analized. Locally, our CPA, chartered a=\nccountants [etc.] will make sure that taxes and social compliance including=\n the payroll&#160;are taken care off. Possibly, with the transfer of the ge=\nneral ledger and the trial balance kept on the company's group system, they=\n will either check the compliance or check the audit accordingly to the app=\nlicable national standard.</p>=0D=0A=0D=0A=0D=0A=0A\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>=0A=0A\t\t\t\t\t<=\ndiv style=3D\"clear:both;\">=0A\t\t\t\t\t&nbsp;=0A\t\t\t\t\t</div>=0A\t\t</div>=0A\t\t</div>=\n=0A  </div>=0A=0A\t<div style=3D\"text-align:center;position:relative;top:10p=\nx;font-size:10px;\">=0A\t\tConstantin - Serval &amp; Associes Copyright 2011 |=\n <a href=3D\"/locations\">Contact us</a> | <a href=3D\"/pages/usefuladdresses\"=\n>Useful addresses</a>| <a href=3D\"/users/sign_in\">Login</a>=0A\t</div>=0A\t<d=\niv style=3D\"padding:20px;color:#8B8C8E;font-size:11px;\">=0A\t=0A\t</div>=0A</=\ndiv>=0A<script type=3D\"text/javascript\">=0Avar gaJsHost =3D ((\"https:\" =3D=\n=3D document.location.protocol) ? composed of Jean-Fran=C3=A7ois Serva=\nl, International partner, M. Daniel Nagle, US Managing Director. For New Yo=\nrk State CPA firm, partners are Adriana Agbo and Jean-Fran=C3=A7ois Serval.=\n</p>=0D=0A<h4>Governance process</h4>=0D=0A<p>The network member firms&#160=\n;is linked by contract. This contract commits member firms and all of their=\n partners to technical reviews and governance process on all aspects of the=\nir practice and behavior. An independent oversight body is in charge of dea=\nling with open issues.</p>=0D=0A<h4>Processes</h4>=0D=0A<div>Constantin - S=\nerval &amp; Associes's organization is also set up to allow <strong>complia=\nnce</strong> with International Federation of Accountants \"IFAC\" <em>code o=\nf Ethics</em> and other major National code of Ethics and professional proc=\nurements. This organization is transparent to competent authorities.</div>=\n=0D=0A<p>At the same time, all necessary processes are implemented to prote=\nct the client's data and <strong>privacy</strong>.</p>=0D=0A<h4>Quality con=\ntrol</h4>=0D=0A<p>Constantin - Serval &amp; Associes is organized in order =\nto comply with all regulation rules of Ethics through assigned executives u=\nsing specific global software in order to mesure&#160;the risk&#160;of the =\nassigments, the absence of conflict of interest and the quality of the work=\n performed. <br />A compliance officer is in charge of the correct implemen=\ntation of the processes. Quality controls are performed with internal resou=\nres as well as outside resources.</p>=0D=0A<h4>International Coordination</=\nh4>=0D=0A<p>M Jean-Fran=C3=A7ois Serval, a French CPA and UK Auditor, is co=\nordinating assignments with head offices and other US or foreign internatio=\nnal practices. <br />Through its branch offices and correspondents, Constan=\ntin - Serval &amp; Associes network -now covering all of western europe, no=\nrth america and northern africa-  is able to service its clientele internat=\nionally.</p>=0D=0A<h4>Network</h4>=0D=0A<p>The network is not only organize=\nd in order to have the Member Firms complying with the professional<span> g=\nuidance=E2=80=99s (IFAC=E2=80=A6and others), laws and regulations but also =\nto wholly implement specific rules decided to ensure dedication of staff an=\nd quality of work with quality control as well as security for clients if a=\n difficulty arises on an assignment. Processes are also set to ensure long =\nterm consistency of the network as well as a sanction process if a partner =\nis not respecting the rules. The network also has governance global bodies =\nin place to implement its rules. <br />The Member Firms are those which hav=\ne signed the network framework agreement contract dealing with the above ma=\ntters and goals.<br /> <br />The Correspondent Firms are those which are cu=\nrrently practicing or working with Constantin/Groupe Audit- Serval &amp; As=\nsoci=C3=A9s network without having signed the network framework agreement. =\nLike the Member Firms, they have to comply with all rules and professional =\nprocurements applicable for the assignments as well as to justify the absen=\nce of conflict and their independence. <br />None of the both status consid=\ners the existence or the possibility of referral fees between the firms. I=\nnstruments</h1>=0A<p>FASB has published an exposure draft about Fair market=\n value \"FMV\"&nbsp;and comprehensive income.</p>=0D=0A<p>It clarifies how FM=\nV could be used for financial instruments valuation and consider that both =\n\"FMV\" and amortized cost should be used and reconciled.</p>=0D=0A<p>The pro=\nject corresponds very closely to our papers available in the \"publications\"=\n space.</p>=0D=0A<p>We believe that this project is a big improvement compa=\nred with IASB 3&nbsp;phases project. Nevertheless, we consider that \"FMV\" v=\naluations and effects on P &amp; L are too sensitive to interest rates and =\nmarket volatility that are out of the bankers scoope of power &nbsp;to be r=\netained as having an effect on the equity in the books that they would be r=\nesponsable of or would react with individual policies that will jeopardize =\nthe global&nbsp;efficiency of the economy&nbsp;. <h3>Publications</h3>=0A  <p><a href=3D\"/publica=\ntions\" >Back to the publications list</a></p>=0A</div>=0A=0A\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>=0A=\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div id=3D\"left_col\">=0A\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<h1>Proposals for a reform of accounti=\nng standards</h1>=0A<p>The attached memo has been written in the context of=\n the 2007 financial crisis that has not yet ended. It criticizes the fair V=\nalue accounting standard as a criminal approach that allowed to inflate bal=\nance sheets to feed the intermediation of brokers of financial papers and t=\nhe all the financial community with the silent complicity of those, includi=\nng governments who wanted to issue debts to postpone the required balancing=\n of budgets.  The crash with tendencies to deflation was the result of this=\n standard when the cash flows and money rotation (needed for money markets)=\n were not to justify the posted in the balance sheets values (subprime=E2=\n=80=A6). The proposition is to go back to historical cost accounting with e=\nstimates by categories of instruments (depending on warrantees, issuers and=\n duration) to be added and computed as potential adjustments to the equity =\n(comprehensive income) but not as a mean of proof for the judges. More deta=\nils were given in the book and in various speeches given in Washington in 2=\n011 and 2012 at the NYSE. Contents of these public speeches are available o=\nn demand.</p>=0A<br />=0A<div class=3D\"box\">=0A  <ul>=0A  <li>=0A\t\t<a href=\n=3D\"/publications/order\">Order this publication</a>=0A\t</li>=0A\t</ul>=0A</d=\niv>=0A<br /><br />=0A=0A=0A\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>=0A=0A\t\t\t\t\t<div style=3D\"clear:both;=\n\">=0A\t\t\t\t\t&nbsp;=0A\t\t\t\t\t</div>=0A\t\t</div>=0A\t\t</div>=0A  </div>=0A=0A\t<div =\nstyle=3D\"text-align:center;position:relative;top:10px;font-size:10px;\">=0A\t=\n\tConstantin - Serval &amp; Associes Copyright 2011 | <a href=3D\"/locations\"=\n>Contact us</a> | <a href=3D\"/pages/usefuladdresses\">Useful addresses</a>| =\n<a href=3D\"/users/sign_in\">Login</a>=0A\t</div>=0A\t<div style=3D\"padding:20p=\nx;color:#8B8C8E;font-size:11px;\">=0A\t=0A\t</div>=0A</div>=0A<script type=3D\"=\ntext/javascript\">=0Avar gaJsHost =3D ((\"https:\" =3D=3D document.location.pr=\notocol) ? list</a></p>=0A</div>=0A=0A\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>=0A\t\t\t\t\t\t<div id=3D\"left_col\">=0A=\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<h1>A new approach to audit</h1>=0A=0D=0A=0D=0A=0D=0A=0D=0A=0D=0A=0D=\n=0A=0D=0A=0D=0A=0D=0A<p>This leaflet explains why audit approaches should b=\ne reviewed for all companies and not only listed ones submitted to section =\n404 of SOX. The reasoning for that is that accounting standards, so far, ma=\ny hide basic phenomena and among the criticized ones is the \"Fair Market Va=\nlue\" of US GAAP n=C2=B0157 (or n=C2=B039 of IFRS). This text was written be=\nfore the financial crisis and appears now as prophetic. It recommends that =\npracticed audits processes (US GAAS or International ISA's) go back to basi=\nc as they are already set for. They should be focused and the reports shoul=\nd be representing how the reporting system is organized and operated in ord=\ner to ensure that all transactions are going into it, whether the processin=\ng of the resulting data is secure and consistently restitutes those data, w=\nhether the accounting aggregates are sensible for the management and meanin=\ngful from a business standpoint before referring to any accounting standard=\n, and finally, whether the bridges to financials are correct enough to have=\n financials compliant to the chosen accounting standards or any applicable =\nor requested reporting formats by authorities. The text reminds what the hi=\nerarchy of the duties to be fulfilled by auditors should be. The innovation=\n is that efficiency in terms of use and quality comes before compliancy lik=\ne principles should come before rules. It explicively states that accountin=\ng standards are just a language and have never any universality. They will =\nlike the Fair Market Value become wrong at a time and that audits should no=\nt rely on them to get appropriateness.<br />You can download the document i=\nn English and also in French.</p>=0A<br />=0A<div class=3D\"box\">=0A  <ul>=\n=0A  <li>=0A\t\t<a href=3D\"/publications/order\">Order this publication</a>=0A=\n\t</li>=0A\t</ul>=0A</div>=0A<br /><br />=0A=0A=0A\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>=0A=0A\t\t\t\t\t<div=\n style=3D\"clear:both;\">=0A\t\t\t\t\t&nbsp;=0A\t\t\t\t\t</div>=0A\t\t</div>=0A\t\t</div>=\n=0A  </div>=0A=0A\t<div style=3D\"text-align:center;position:relative;top:10p=\nx;font-size:10px;\">=0A\t\tConstantin - Serval &amp; Associes Copyright 2011 |=\n <a href=3D\"/locations\">Contact us</a> | <a href=3D\"/pages/usefuladdresses\"=\n>Useful addresses</a>| <a href=3D\"/users/sign_in\">Login</a>=0A\t</div>=0A\t<d=\niv style=3D\"padding:20px;color:#8B8C8E;font-size:11px;\">=0A\t=0A\t</div>=0A</=\ndiv>=0A<script type=3D\"text/javascript\">=0Avar gaJsHost =3D ((\"https:\" =3D=\n=3D document.location.protocol) ?
